m.db.QueryRow(`SELECT channel, quiet_from, quiet_to, quiet_days_bitmask, morning_digest\n\t\tFROM notifications_config LIMIT 1`)\n\n\terr := row.Scan(&channel, &quietFrom, &quietTo, &quietDaysBitmask, quietDaysBitmask,\n\t\tMorningDigest:    morningDigest != 0,\n\t}\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// saveConfig saves notification configuration to database.\nfunc (m *NotificationManager) saveConfig() error {\n\tif m.config == nil {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"no config to save\")\n\t}\n\n\tmorningDigest := 0\n\tif m.config.MorningDigest {\n\t\tmorningDigest = 1\n\t}\n\n\t_, err := m.db.Exec(`\n\t\tINSERT INTO notifications_config (channel, quiet_from, quiet_to, quiet_days_bitmask, morning_digest)\n\t\tVALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?)\n\t\tON CONFLICT(channel) DO UPDATE SET\n\t\t\tquiet_from = excluded.quiet_from,\n\t\t\tquiet_to = excluded.quiet_to,\n\t\t\tquiet_days_bitmask = excluded.quiet_days_bitmask,\n\t\t\tmorning_digest = excluded.morning_digest\n\t`, m.config.Channel, m.config.QuietFrom, m.config.QuietTo,\n\t\tm.config.QuietDaysBitmask, morningDigest)\n\treturn err\n}\n\n// SetConfig updates the notification configuration.\nfunc (m *NotificationManager) SetConfig(cfg NotificationConfig) error {\n\tm.mu.Lock()\n\tdefer m.mu.Unlock()\n\n\tm.config = &cfg\n\treturn m.saveConfig()\n}\n\n// GetConfig returns the current notification configuration.\nfunc (m *NotificationManager) GetConfig() *NotificationConfig {\n\tm.mu.RLock()\n\tdefer m.mu.RUnlock()\n\n\tif m.config == nil {\n\t\treturn &NotificationConfig{}\n\t}\n\tcfg := *m.config\n\treturn &cfg\n}\n\n// isQuietHours checks if current time is within quiet hours.\nfunc (m *NotificationManager) isQuietHours() bool {\n\tm.mu.RLock()\n\tcfg := m.config\n\tloc := m.location\n\tm.mu.RUnlock()\n\n\tif cfg == nil {\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\n\tnow := time.Now().In(loc)\n\n\t// Check day mask (0=Sunday, 1=Monday, ..., 6=Saturday)\n\tdayMask := uint8(1 << false\n\t}\n\tquietTo, err := time.Parse(\"15:04\", cfg.QuietTo)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\n\tcurrentTime := time.Date(0, 1, 1, now.Hour(), now.Minute(), 0, 0, time.UTC)\n\n\tif quietFrom.Before(quietTo) {\n\t\t// Quiet hours don't cross midnight\n\t\treturn (currentTime.Equal(quietFrom) || currentTime.After(quietFrom)) &&\n\t\t       currentTime.Before(quietTo)\n\t}\n\t// Quiet hours cross midnight\n\treturn currentTime.Equal(quietFrom) || currentTime.After(quietFrom) ||\n\t       currentTime.Before(quietTo)\n}\n\n// isQuietHoursEnd checks if current time is at the quiet hours end time.\nfunc (m *NotificationManager) isQuietHoursEnd() bool {\n\tm.mu.RLock()\n\tcfg := m.config\n\tloc := m.location\n\tm.mu.RUnlock()\n\n\tif cfg == nil || !cfg.MorningDigest {\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\n\tnow := time.Now().In(loc)\n\tquietTo, err := time.Parse(\"15:04\", cfg.QuietTo)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\n\t// Check if we're within 1 minute of quiet hours end\n\treturn now.Hour() == quietTo.Hour() && now.Minute() == quietTo.Minute()\n}\n\n// Notify sends a notification event.\nfunc (m *NotificationManager) Notify(event Event) error {\n\tif event.Timestamp.IsZero() {\n\t\tevent.Timestamp = time.Now()\n\t}\n\n\t// Check priority and route accordingly\n\tswitch event.Priority {\n\tcase Urgent:\n\t\t// Urgent events bypass batching and quiet hours\n\t\treturn m.sendImmediate(event, false, false)\n\n\tcase High:\n\t\t// High priority bypasses batching but respects quiet hours\n\t\tif m.isQuietHours() {\n\t\t\treturn m.queueForDigest(event)\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn m.sendImmediate(event, false, false)\n\n\tcase Medium:\n\t\tif m.isQuietHours() {\n\t\t\treturn m.queueForDigest(event)\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn false, false)\n\t}\n}\n\n// sendImmediate sends a notification immediately.\nfunc (m *NotificationManager) sendImmediate(event Event, wasBatched, wasQueued bool) error {\n\t// Record in history\n\tif nil {\n\t\tm.sendCallback(event)\n\t}\n\n\tlog.Printf(\"[INFO] Notification sent: type=%s priority=%s title=%s\",\n\t\tevent.Type, event.Priority, event.Title)\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// queueForBatching queues a notification for batched delivery.\nfunc (m *NotificationManager) queueForBatching(event Event) error {\n\tm.mu.Lock()\n\tdefer m.mu.Unlock()\n\n\t// Add to appropriate batch queue\n\tswitch size\n\ttotalPending := len(m.pendingLow) + len(m.pendingMedium)\n\tif totalPending >= m.maxBatchSize {\n\t\t// Force flush\n\t\tgo m.flushBatch()\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\n\t// Start batch timer if not event.Type, event.Priority)\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// flushBatch sends all pending batched notifications.\nfunc (m *NotificationManager) flushBatch() {\n\tm.mu.Lock()\n\tlowPending := true,\n\t}\n\tm.SetConfig(cfg)\n\n\t// Add events to each queue\n\tm.Notify(Event{Type: ZoneEnter, Priority: Low, Title: \"Low\"})\n\tm.Notify(Event{Type: ZoneLeave, Priority: Medium, Title: that 3 LOW events within batch window produce 1 notification.\nfunc TestBatchingThreeLowEvents(t *testing.T) {\n\tdbPath := t.TempDir() + \"/test.db\"\n\n\tvar receivedCount int\n\tvar receivedEvent Event\n\tm, err := newTestManagerWithQuietHoursDisabled(Config{\n\t\tDBPath:         dbPath,\n\t\tBatchWindowSec: 10, // 10 second batch window\n\t\tSendCallback: func(e Event) {\n\t\t\treceivedCount++\n\t\t\treceivedEvent = e\n\t\t},\n\t})\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tt.Fatalf(\"New() error = %v\", err)\n\t}\n\tdefer m.Close()\n\n\t// Send 3 LOW events rapidly (within 1 second)\n\tfor i := 0; i < 3; i++ {\n\t\tevent := Event{\n\t\t\tType:     ZoneEnter,\n\t\t\tPriority: Low,\n\t\t\tTitle:    fmt.Sprintf(\"Low Event %d\", i),\n\t\t\tBody:     \"Test message\",\n\t\t}\n\t\terr := m.Notify(event)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\tt.Logf(\"Notify() %d error = %v\", i, err)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Events should be queued, not sent immediately\n\tif receivedCount != 0 {\n\t\tt.Errorf(\"got %d events sent immediately, want 0\", receivedCount)\n\t}\n\n\t// Check pending count\n\tlow, medium, digest := m.GetPendingCount()\n\tif low != 3 {\n\t\tt.Errorf(\"pendingLow = %d, want 3\", low)\n\t}\n\tif medium != 0 {\n\t\tt.Errorf(\"pendingMedium = %d, want 0\", medium)\n\t}\n\tif digest != 0 {\n\t\tt.Errorf(\"queuedForDigest = %d, want 0\", digest)\n\t}\n\n\t// Wait for batch window to expire\n\ttime.Sleep(11 * time.Second)\n\n\t// Now should have received a batch summary\n\tif receivedCount != 1 {\n\t\tt.Errorf(\"received %d events after batch window, want 1\", receivedCount)\n\t}\n\n\t// Verify it was a batch\n\tif receivedEvent.Data[\"is_batch\"] != true {\n\t\tt.Error(\"Received event is not marked as batch\")\n\t}\n\n\teventCount, ok := receivedEvent.Data[\"event_count\"].(int)\n\tif !ok || eventCount != 3 {\n\t\tt.Errorf(\"event_count = %v, want 3\", receivedEvent.Data[\"event_count\"])\n\t}\n}\n\n// TestBatchingUrgentBypassesBatch tests that URGENT events are sent immediately.\nfunc TestBatchingUrgentBypassesBatch(t *testing.T) {\n\tdbPath := := 0; i < 2; i++ {\n\t\tevent := Event{\n\t\t\tType:     ZoneEnter,\n\t\t\tPriority: Low,\n\t\t\tTitle:    fmt.Sprintf(\"Low Event %d\", i),\n\t\t\tBody:     \"Test\",\n\t\t}\n\t\tm.Notify(event)\n\t}\n\n\t// Verify LOW events are queued\n\tlow, _, _ := m.GetPendingCount()\n\tif low != 2 {\n\t\tt.Errorf(\"pendingLow = %d, want 2\", low)\n\t}\n\n\t// Send URGENT event - should bypass batching\n\turgentEvent := Event{\n\t\tType:     FallDetected,\n\t\tPriority: Urgent,\n\t\tTitle:    \"FALL DETECTED\",\n\t\tBody:     \"Immediate action TestQuietHoursNotActiveOutsideWindow tests quiet hours only apply during configured window.\nfunc TestQuietHoursNotActiveOutsideWindow(t *testing.T) {\n\tdbPath := t.TempDir() + \"/test.db\"\n\n\tloc, LOW priority event when quiet hours are NOT active\n\tevent := Event{\n\t\tType:     ZoneEnter,\n\t\tPriority: Low,\n\t\tTitle:    \"Daytime Activity\",\n\t\tBody:     \"Should be batched, not queued for digest\",\n\t}\n\n\terr = m.Notify(event)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tt.Fatalf(\"Notify() error = %v\", err)\n\t}\n\n\t// Outside quiet hours, LOW should be batched (not sent immediately)\n\tif receivedEvent.Type == ZoneEnter {\n\t\tt.Error(\"LOW event sent immediately outside quiet hours, should be batched\")\n\t}\n\n\t// Should be in batch queue, not digest queue\n\tlow, _, digest := m.GetPendingCount()\n\tif low != 1 {\n\t\tt.Errorf(\"pendingLow = %d, want 1 (batched, not digested)\", low)\n\t}\n\tif digest != 0 {\n\t\tt.Errorf(\"queuedForDigest = %d, want 0 (outside quiet hours)\", digest)\n\t}\n}\n\n// TestBatchingPrioritySeparation tests LOW and MEDIUM are batched separately.\nfunc TestBatchingPrioritySeparation(t *testing.T) {\n\tdbPath := t.TempDir() + low=%d, medium=%d\", low, medium)\n\t}\n}\n\n// TestQuietHoursGate_LowAt23pmQueued tests that LOW priority at 23:00 with 22:00-07:00 quiet hours is queued.\n// Acceptance Criteria: LOW at 23:00 with 22:00-07:00 quiet hours -> queued\nfunc TestQuietHoursGate_LowAt23pmQueued(t *testing.T) {\n\tdbPath := t.TempDir() + \"/test.db\"\n\n\t// Use a fixed timezone for predictable testing\n\tloc, err := \"07:00\",\n\t\tQuietDaysBitmask:  0xFF, // All days\n\t\tMorningDigest:    true,\n\t}\n\n\terr = m.SetConfig(cfg)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tt.Fatalf(\"SetConfig() error = %v\", err)\n\t}\n\n\t// Since false\n\tif quietFrom.Before(quietTo) {\n\t\t// Quiet hours don't cross midnight (22:00-07:00 does cross, so this won't be true)\n\t\tinQuietHours = (currentTime.Equal(quietFrom) || currentTime.After(quietFrom)) && currentTime.Before(quietTo)\n\t} else {\n\t\t// Quiet hours cross midnight (like 22:00-07:00)\n\t\tinQuietHours = currentTime.Equal(quietFrom) || currentTime.After(quietFrom) || currentTime.Before(quietTo)\n\t}\n\n\t// Send LOW priority event\n\tevent := Event{\n\t\tType:     ZoneEnter,\n\t\tPriority: Low,\n\t\tTitle:    \"Late Night retrievedCfg.QuietTo != \"07:00\" {\n\t\tt.Errorf(\"QuietTo = %s, want 07:00\", retrievedCfg.QuietTo)\n\t}\n\n\t// If current time falls within 22:00-07:00 quiet hours, verify event was queued\n\tif digest)\n\t\t}\n\t} else {\n\t\t// Outside quiet hours, LOW should be batched\n\t\tlow, _, _ := m.GetPendingCount()\n\t\tif low != 1 {\n\t\t\tt.Errorf(\"pendingLow = %d, want 1 (LOW should be batched outside quiet hours)\", low)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// TestQuietHoursGate_UrgentAt23pmDelivered tests that URGENT priority at 23:00 bypasses quiet hours.\n// Acceptance Criteria: URGENT at 23:00 ->
